         linkTrack('socialLinkClick');
     }
     function helpdeskQuery(helpdeskQuery1, helpdeskQuery2) {
         digitalData.eventData = {
             helpdeskQuery1: helpdeskQuery1,
             helpdeskQuery2: helpdeskQuery2
         }
         linkTrack('helpdeskQuery');
     }
     function createQuote(cartID) {
         digitalData.eventData = {
             cartID: cartID
         }
         linkTrack('createQuote');
     }
     function refundNReplace(orderID, orderPrice) {
         digitalData.eventData = {
             orderID: orderID,
             orderPrice: orderPrice
         }
         linkTrack('refundNReplace');
     }
   </script>

             var script = document.createElement('script');
             script.type = "text/javascript";

                     document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0].appendChild(script);

    <script>
     function func_subscribe() {
             $("#subscribetoemail").prop("disabled", true);
             var vemailaddress = $("#input-signup-email").val();
             $.ajax({
                 type: "POST",
                 url: '/scripts/mailing_list_add.asp',
                 data: "email_address=" + vemailaddress + "&leadsource=2",
                 success: function (result) {
                     linkTrack('emailSubscription');
                     //$("#mp-footer-email-form").css('display', 'none');
                     $("#mp-footer-email-message").css('display', 'block');
                     $("#mp-footer-email-message").html(result);
                     $("#subscribetoemail").prop("disabled", false);
                 },
                 error: function () {
                     $("#subscribetoemail").prop("disabled", false);
                     return true;
                 }
             });
 
             return false;
         }
    </script>
